(reset! new-session)

Mutates the session from a :then block.

Source

(defn reset! "Mutates the session from a :then block." [new-session] (if *mutable-session* (if (= *session* @*mutable-session*) (vreset! *mutable-session* new-session) (throw (ex-info "You may only call `reset!` once in a :then block" {}))) (throw (ex-info "You may only call `reset!` in a :then block" {}))))
